Even the lobby has high speed internet Internal Features - A high ceiling. I feel liberated by the high ceiling design and the place definitely looked bigger and more spacious in person - Sleek and modern furniture. - A complete collection of cooking wares - High speed internet - High quality sheets and pillows (Memory form FTW) - Washer and dryer!
